A significant proportion of the health care delivery capacity in #Africa lies within #faith-based institutions ‚Äì in some places accounting for 30-70%.
The #faith-based community was in #Africa long before the #HIV epidemic began and it will be there long after the epidemic is controlled. We must invest in faith-based institutions and #faith leaders for impact and sustainability.
We invest in #faith-based institutions and #faith leaders not only to reach the populations we are missing in the #HIV response and accelerate progress toward controlling the pandemic but also to ensure our efforts last far into the future.
#Faith-based organizations and #faith leaders are critical partners in controlling the #HIV pandemic, often having unique relationships of trust with communities and individuals that are not always easily replicated by the public health sector.
Since 2015, @PEPFAR and @UNAIDS have co-led the Faith Initiative, which strengthens the capacity of #faith-based leaders and organizations to advocate for and deliver a sustainable #HIV response.
.@PEPFAR supports nearly 1 million #children on lifesaving #HIV #treatment. We continue to invest nearly half a billion dollars annually, including through #faith-based organizations, to ensure children are prioritized.  Learn more: https://t.co/APy44ThwL6 https://t.co/PFaFt5DkQC
The faith community helps us in reaching individuals who are not often accessed by our traditional public health systems and in reducing stigma and discrimination. - @MichelSidibe @UNAIDS https://t.co/akjgLBCkno

We understand our obligation. Our job is to find and serve those who we are missing, including children. The faith community is vital to #EndAIDS and #EndTB. - #AmbBirx https://t.co/WUYY3uQfzF

RT @MichelSidibe: We can‚Äôt afford to miss opportunity @PEPFAR Amb Birx has outlined for integrating #TB #HIV testing and treatment and we k‚Ä¶
The number of people living with #HIV who initiated #TB preventive therapy with @PEPFAR support increased from 10,000 in 2014 to more than 880,000 in 2017, with TPT completion rates reaching 90% in most settings. #UNGA #HLM
Combining #TB preventative therapy and #HIV treatment has been shown to reduce the risk of TB disease by almost 95%; TB preventative therapy has been shown to reduce mortality in people living with HIV by 37%, independent of ART and CD4 cell count. #UNGA #HLM
By emphasizing routine screening for the symptoms of #TB disease in all people living with #HIV at every visit to a @PEPFAR-supported facility, we're better able to find TB disease early and refer directly for treatment. #UNGA #HLM
Expanding access to life-saving antiretroviral treatment is the cornerstone of @PEPFAR‚Äôs #TB/#HIV efforts. Early ART protects the immune system and prevents opportunistic infections including TB. #UNGA #HLM
Our #TB-#HIV priorities: 1) testing TB cases for HIV &amp; treating both infections, 2) treating for HIV before immune system damage increases TB risk, &amp; 3) screening HIV+ clients for TB, curing them if diagnosed or providing TB preventive therapy. #HLM #UNGA @CDCGlobal @USAID
